<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t0" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">1.  简介</span></span></p>

</div>
<p>Hive是基于Hadoop的一个数据仓库工具，可以将结构化的数据文件映射为一张数据库表，并提供完整的sql查询功能，可以将sql语句转换为MapReduce任务进行运行。 其优点是学习成本低，可以通过类SQL语句快速实现简单的MapReduce统计，不必开发专门的MapReduce应用，十分适合数据仓库的统计分析。<br>
</p>
<p>Hive与HBase的整合功能的实现是利用两者本身对外的API接口互相进行通信，相互通信主要是依靠hive_hbase-handler.jar工具类， 大致意思如图所示：</p>
<p><img alt="" src="http://hi.csdn.net/attachment/201202/22/0_13298754602281.gif" style="border:none; max-width:100%"><br>
</p>
<p><br>
</p>
<p></p>
<div>
<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t1" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">2.  <span style="color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)"><strong>Hive项目介绍</strong></span></span></span></p>

</div>
<p></p>
<p></p>
<div class="O1" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; font-weight:bold; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden"><span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">项目结构</span></div>
</div>
<img src="https://img-blog.csdn.net/20140208153547265?watermark/2/text/aHR0cDovL2Jsb2cuY3Nkbi5uZXQvaGd1aXN1/font/5a6L5L2T/fontsize/400/fill/I0JBQkFCMA==/dissolve/70/gravity/Center" alt="" style="border:none; max-width:100%"><br>
</div>
<div class="O" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 
<p><span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">Hive</span>配置文件介绍<br>
</span>•hive-site.xml      hive的配置文件<br>
•hive-env.sh        hive的运行环境文件<br>
•hive-default.xml.template  默认模板<br>
•hive-env.sh.template     hive-env.sh默认配置<br>
•hive-exec-log4j.properties.template   exec默认配置<br>
• hive-log4j.properties.template log默认配置<br>
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">hive</span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">-site.xml<br>
</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">&lt;</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">property&gt;<br>
</span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">  &lt;name&gt;javax.jdo.option.ConnectionURL&lt;/name&gt; </span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">&lt;value&gt;jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/hive?createData</span> <span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">baseIfNotExist=true&lt;/value&gt;<br>
</span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">  &lt;description&gt;JDBC connect string for a JDBC </span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">metastore&lt;/description&gt;<br>
</span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">&lt;/property&gt;<br>
</span>&lt;property&gt;<br>
&lt;name&gt;javax.jdo.option.ConnectionDriverName&lt;/name&gt;<br>
    &lt;value&gt;com.mysql.jdbc.Driver&lt;/value&gt;<br>
  &lt;description&gt;Driver class name for a JDBC metastore&lt;/description&gt;<br>
&lt;/property&gt;<br>
&lt;property&gt;<br>
&lt;name&gt;javax.jdo.option.ConnectionUserName&lt;/name&gt;<br>
    &lt;value&gt;root&lt;/value&gt;<br>
   &lt;description&gt;username to use against metastore database&lt;/description&gt;<br>
&lt;/property&gt;<br>
&lt;property&gt;<br>
&lt;name&gt;javax.jdo.option.ConnectionPassword&lt;/name&gt;<br>
   &lt;value&gt;test&lt;/value&gt;<br>
   &lt;description&gt;password to use against metastore database&lt;/description&gt;<br>
&lt;/property&gt;<br>
  </p>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<p><span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px"><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">hive</span><span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">-env.sh<br>
</span></span>•配置Hive的配置文件路径<br>
•export HIVE_CONF_DIR= your path<br>
•配置Hadoop的安装路径<br>
•HADOOP_HOME=your hadoop home</p>
<p>我们按数据元的存储方式不同安装。</p>
<p><br>
</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t2" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">3.  <span style="color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px"><strong>使用Derby数据库</strong></span>安装</span></span></p>

</div>
<p></p>
<div class="O" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; font-weight:bold">什么是<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">Derby</span>安装方式</span></div>
<div style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•Apache Derby是一个完全用java编写的数据库，所以可以跨平台，但需要在JVM中运行</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•Derby是一个Open source的产品，基于Apache License 2.0分发</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•即将元数据存储在Derby数据库中，也是Hive默认的安装方式</div>
</div>
<p></p>
<p><br>
</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t3" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>1 .Hadoop和Hbase都已经成功安装了</h3>
<p><span class="link_title"></span>Hadoop集群配置：http://blog.csdn.net/hguisu/article/details/723739</p>
<p>hbase安装配置：http://blog.csdn.net/hguisu/article/details/7244413</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t4" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><strong>2. 下载<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; font-size:14px; line-height:22.8500003814697px">hive</span></strong></h3>
<p><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px"><span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px">hive目前最新的版本是0.12，我们先从</span></span><a target="_blank" href="http://mirror.bit.edu.cn/apache/hive/hive-0.12.0/" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">http://mirror.bit.edu.cn/apache/hive/hive-0.12.0/</a><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px"> 上下载</span><a target="_blank" href="http://mirror.bit.edu.cn/apache/hive/hive-0.12.0/hive-0.12.0.tar.gz" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">hive-0.12.0.tar.gz</a><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">，但是请注意，此版本基于是基于hadoop1.3和hbase0.94的（</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px"><span style="color:rgb(204,0,0)">如果安装hadoop2.X
 ，我们需要修改相应的内容）</span></span><br>
</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t5" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>3. <span style="font-family:Simsun; font-size:14px; line-height:19px">安装：</span></h3>
<p><span style="background-color:rgb(51,51,51)"><span style="color:rgb(204,204,204)">tar zxvf hive-0.12.0.tar.gz <br>
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="background-color:rgb(51,51,51)"><span style="color:rgb(204,204,204)"> cd hive-0.12.0</span></span></p>
<p><br>
</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t6" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>4. 替换jar包，与<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; line-height:20px">hbase0.96和hadoop2.2版本一致。</span></h3>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:16px; line-height:20px">   由于我们下载的hive是基于hadoop1.3和hbase0.94的，所以必须进行替换，因为我们的hbse0.96是基于hadoop2.2的，所以我们必须先解决hive的hadoop版本问题，目前我们从官网下载的hive都是用1.几的版本编译的，因此我们需要自己下载源码来用hadoop2.X的版本重新编译hive，这个过程也很简单，只需要如下步骤：</span></div>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:16px; line-height:20px"><br>
</span></div>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:16px"></span>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">    </span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">1. 先从</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'"><a target="_blank" href="http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hive/branches/branch-0.12" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none"><span style="font-size:10.5pt">http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hive/branches/branch-0.12</span></a><span style="font-size:10.5pt"> 或者是<span style="font-size:10.5pt; color:rgb(51,102,153)"><a target="_blank" href="http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hive/branches/branch-0.12" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none">http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hive/trunk</a> 
  我们下载到</span></span></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'">/home/hadoop/branch-0.12下。</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><br>
</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">    2.  <span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:20px"><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0)"><a target="_blank" href="http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hive/branches/branch-0.12" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none">branch-0.12</a>是使用ant编译，trunk下面是使用</span><span style="line-height:21px">maven</span></span>编译，如果未按照maven，需要从</span><a target="_blank" href="http://maven.apache.org/download.cgi" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">http://maven.apache.org/download.cgi</a><span style="font-size:10.5pt"> 下载maven，或者使用yum
 install maven。然后解压出来并在PATH下把$maven_home/bin加入或者使用链接（ln -s /usr/local/bin/mvn $maven_home/bin ）.然后就是使用mvn 命令。</span><span style="font-size:10.5pt">运行mvn -v就能</span><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">知道maven是否配置成功</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> </span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">       3.   配置好maven开始编译hive，我们cd到下载源码的</span><a target="_blank" href="http://svn.apache.org/repos/asf/hive/branches/branch-0.12" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,102,153); text-decoration:none; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; line-height:22.8571434020996px"><span style="font-size:10.5pt">branch-0.12</span></a><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'"> 目录，然后运行</span><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5; color:rgb(255,0,255)">mvn
 clean package -DskipTests -Phadoop-2</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">开始编译</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><br>
</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">    4.编译好后的新jar包是存放在各个模块下的target的，这些新jar包的名字都叫</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'"><span style="font-size:10.5pt">hive-***-0.13.0-SNAPSHOT.jar，***为hive下的模块名，</span></span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">我们需要运行命令将其拷贝到hive-0.12.0/lib下</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">。</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'">    find /home/hadoop/branch-0.12  -name "hive*SNAPSHOT.jar"|xargs -i cp {} /home/hadoop/hive-0.12.0/lib。拷贝过去后我们比照着删除原lib下对应的0.12版本的jar包。</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'"><span style="font-size:10.5pt">  </span></span></div>
<div style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-size:10.5pt; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; line-height:20px">    </span><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'">5. 接着我们同步hbase的版本，先cd到hive0.12.0/lib下，将hive-0.12.0/lib下hbase-0.94开头的那两个jar包删掉，然后从/home/hadoop/</span><span style="line-height:1.5; color:rgb(255,0,0)"><span style="line-height:24px"><span style="font-size:12px">hbase-0.96.0-hadoop2</span></span></span><span style="font-size:14.2857151031494px; line-height:22.8571434020996px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'">/lib下hbase开头的包都拷贝过来</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'">    </span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> </span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">find /home/hadoop/hbase-0.96.0-hadoop/lib
 -name "hbase*.jar"|xargs -i cp {} ./</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><br>
</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">    </span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">6. 基本的同步完成了，重点检查下zookeeper和protobuf的jar包是否和hbase保持一致，如果不一致，</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"></span>
<p>       拷贝<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; line-height:21px">protobuf</span>.**.jar和zookeeper-3.4.5.jar到hive/lib下。</p>
</div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">  </span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">   7.如果用mysql当原数据库，</span></div>
<div style="line-height:20px; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">      别忘了找一个mysql的jdbcjar包</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'">mysql-connector-java-3.1.12-bin.jar也拷贝到hive-0.12.0/lib下</span></div>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t7" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>5. 配置hive</h3>
</div>
<div>
<div class="O1" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•进入hive-0.12/conf目录</div>
<div class="O1" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•依据hive-env.sh.template，创建hive-env.sh文件</div>
<div class="O2" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•cp  hive-env.sh.template hive-env.sh</div>
<div class="O1" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•修改hive-env.sh</div>
<div class="O2" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•指定hive配置文件的路径</div>
<div class="O3" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•export HIVE_CONF_DIR=/home/hadoop/hive-0.12/conf</div>
<div class="O2" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•指定Hadoop路径</div>
<div class="O3" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
• HADOOP_HOME=/home/hadoop/hadoop-2.2.0</div>
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div></div>
<br>
<p></p>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><span style="background-color:rgb(250,250,250)">H</span>ive使用Hadoop，这意味着你必须在PATH里面设置了hadoop路径，或者导出export HADOOP_HOME=&lt;hadoop-install-dir&gt;也可以。</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">另外，你必须在创建Hive库表前，在HDFS上创建/tmp和/hive/warehousedir（也称为hive.metastore.warehouse.dir的），并且将它们的权限设置为chmod g+w。完成这个操作的命令如下：</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">$ $HADOOP_HOME/bin/hadoop fs -mkdir /tmp</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">$ $HADOOP_HOME/bin/hadoop fs -mkdir /hive/warehousedir</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">$ $HADOOP_HOME/bin/hadoop fs -chmod g+w /tmp</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">$ $HADOOP_HOME/bin/hadoop fs -chmod g+w/hive/warehousedir</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">    我同样发现设置HIVE_HOME是很重要的，但并非必须。</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">$ export HIVE_HOME=&lt;hive-install-dir&gt;</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">    在Shell中使用Hive命令行(cli)模式：</span><br style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">$ $HIVE_HOME/bin/hive</span></div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"></span>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t8" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>5. 启动hive</h3>
<p><strong>1）.单节点启动</strong></p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)"><code class="plain" style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">#bin/hive -hiveconf hbase.master=master:490001</code></span><br>
</p>
<p><strong>2） 集群启动：</strong></p>
<p style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)"><span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)"><code class="plain">#bin/hive -hiveconf hbase.zookeeper.quorum=node1,node2,node3</code></span></p>
<p><code class="plain">如何hive-site.xml文件中没有配置hive.aux.jars.path，则可以按照如下方式启动。</code></p>
<p><code class="plain"><code class="plain">bin/hive --auxpath /usr/local/hive/lib/hive-hbase-handler-</code><code class="value">0.96</code><code class="plain">.</code><code class="value">0</code><code class="plain">.jar, /usr/local/hive/lib/hbase-</code><code class="value">0.96</code><code class="plain">.jar,
 /usr/local/hive/lib/zookeeper-</code><code class="value">3.3</code><code class="plain">.</code><code class="value">2</code><code class="plain">.jar -hiveconf hbase.zookeeper.quorum=node1,node2,node3</code></code></p>
启动直接#bin/hive 也可以。</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"></span>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t9" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>6 测试hive</h3>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•建立测试表pokes</div>
<div class="O1" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
hive&gt; CREATE TABLE pokes (foo INT, bar STRING);<br>
OK<br>
Time taken: 1.842 seconds<br>
hive&gt; show tables;                             <br>
OK<br>
pokes<br>
Time taken: 0.182 seconds, Fetched: 1 row(s)<br>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
 </div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
•数据导入pokes<br>
<span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)"><span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">hive&gt; LOAD DATA LOCAL INPATH './examples/files/kv1.txt' OVERWRITE INTO pokse</span></span><br>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)"><span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)"><br>
</span></span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">然后查看hadoop的文件：</span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
bin/hadoop dfs -ls /hive/warehousedir<br>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
看到新增一个文件：</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
drwxr-xr-x   - hadoop supergroup     0  09:06 /hive/warehousedir/pokes</div>
</div>
<br>
<p><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">注：使用derby存储方式时，运行hive会在当前目录生成</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:yellow">一个</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:yellow">derby</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:yellow">文件</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">和</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:yellow">一个</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:yellow">metastore_db</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:yellow">目录</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">。这种存储方式的</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; background-color:red">弊端</span><span style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">是在同一个目录下同时只能有一个hive客户端能使用数据库，否则报错。</span></p>
<p><br>
</p>
<h1 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t10" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
<div></div>
</h1>
<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">4.  使用MYSQL数据库的方式安装</span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<p><span style="font-weight:normal"><span class="bold" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">安装<span lang="EN-US" style="padding:0px; margin:0px">MySQL<br>
</span></span>• Ubuntu 采用apt-get安装<br>
• sudo apt-get install mysql-server<br>
• 建立数据库hive<br>
• create database hivemeta<br>
• 创建hive用户,并授权<br>
• grant all on hive.* to hive@'%'  identified by 'hive';  <br>
• flush privileges;  </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight:normal">我们直接修改<span style="font-size:14px"><strong>hive-site.xml就可以啦。</strong></span></span></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">

<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-weight:normal">其中<span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)">hiveMeta</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)">是mysql的数据库名</span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)">。</span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif"><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); line-height:20px">createDatabaseIfNotExist</span></span><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">没有就自动创建</span></span></div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<br>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t14" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>本地mysql启动hive ：</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t15" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><span style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; font-weight:normal"><br>
</span></h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t16" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><span style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px; font-weight:normal">直接运行#bin/hive 就可以。</span></h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px"><span style="white-space:pre; font-weight:normal; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)"></span></span>

</div>

</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t17" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>远端mysql方式，启动hive：</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t18" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><span style="font-family:verdana,sans-serif; font-size:13px; line-height:17px"><br>
</span></h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t19" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><span style="font-family:verdana,sans-serif; font-size:13px; line-height:17px">服务器端（192.168.1.214上机master上）：</span></h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-family:verdana,sans-serif; font-size:13px; line-height:17px"><br>
</span></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t20" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><span style="font-family:verdana,sans-serif; font-size:13px; line-height:17px">     在服务器端启动一个 MetaStoreServer，客户端利用 Thrift
 协议通过 MetaStoreServer 访问元数据库。</span></h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div></div>
</div>
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">   启动hive，这个又可以分为启动metastore和hiveserver，其中metastore用于和mysql之间的表结构创建或更新时通讯，hiveserver用于客户端连接，这这个都要启动，具体的启动命令：</span></div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<div><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">启动metastore：</span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)"><strong>hive --service metastore  </strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> </span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><strong>-hiveconf
 hbase.zookeeper.quorum=node1,<strong>node2，<strong>node3</strong></strong> -hiveconf hbase.zookeeper.property.clientPort=2222</strong></span><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5; color:rgb(255,0,0)"> </span><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">（远程mysql需要启动）</span></div>
<div><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><br>
</span></div>
<div>启动hiveservice：<span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)"><strong>hive --service hiveserver </strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> </span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><strong>-hiveconf
 hbase.zookeeper.quorum=</strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255)"></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); line-height:21px"><strong>node1,</strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); line-height:21px"><strong>node2，node3 </strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><strong> -hiveconf
 hbase.zookeeper.property.clientPort=2222</strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> (启动服务，这样jdbc:hive就能连上，默认10000端口，后面的部分一定要带上，否则用eclipse连接不上的)</span></div>
</div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> 起来后我们在eclipse就可以使用jdbc:hive来连接了。如</span></div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<div><span style="font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">    </span><span style="font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">    </span><span style="color:windowtext; font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5">Class.</span><span style="color:windowtext; font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5"><em>forName</em></span><span style="color:windowtext; font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5">(</span><span style="font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5; color:rgb(42,0,255)">"org.apache.hadoop.hive.jdbc.HiveDriver"</span><span style="color:windowtext; font-family:'Courier New'; font-size:12pt; line-height:1.5">);</span></div>
<div><span style="font-size:12pt; color:windowtext; font-family:'Courier New'">        <span style="color:rgb(255,0,128)"><strong>Connection</strong></span> conn = DriverManager.<span style="font-style:italic">getConnection</span>(<span style="color:rgb(42,0,255)">"jdbc:hive://server1:10000/hiveMeta"</span>,<span style="color:rgb(42,0,255)">"root"</span>,<span style="color:rgb(42,0,255)">"111111"</span>);</span></div>
<span style="font-size:12pt; color:windowtext; font-family:'Courier New'">        <span style="color:rgb(127,0,85)"><strong>return</strong></span> conn;</span></div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px">其实使用上和普通的数据库已经很相似了，除了建表的语句有一些差别。</span></div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"><br>
</span></div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"></span>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px">当然你也可以在hive-0.12.0/bin运行</span></div>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">hive  </span><span style="color:rgb(0,0,255); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5">-hiveconf hive.root.logger=DEBUG,console</span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"> </span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><strong>-hiveconf
 hbase.zookeeper.quorum=</strong></span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255)">server2,server3</span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><strong> -hiveconf hbase.zookeeper.property.clientPort=2222</strong></span></div>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:1.5"><strong><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255)"><strong>其中 hbase.zookeeper.property.clientPort</strong></span><strong>就是hbase-site.xml配置的zookeeper的端口号。</strong><br>
</strong></span></div>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><br>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</h3>
<h5 style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t21" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>客户端hive 的<span style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-size:14px; line-height:21px">hive-site.xml</span><span style="font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-weight:normal">配置文件：</span></h5>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"></span>

<span style="font-weight:normal"><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">这一步，我们新加了配置</span></span></div>
<div class="O" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; font-weight:bold; line-height:21px; padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<span style="font-weight:normal"><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px"><span style="color:rgb(51,102,255)">&lt;property&gt;
  <br>
  &lt;name&gt;hive.metastore.uris&lt;/name&gt;  <br>
  &lt;value&gt;thrift://192.168.1.214:9083&lt;/value&gt;  <br>
&lt;/property&gt;  </span></span></span></div>
</div>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"><span style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif; line-height:21px">这个就是使用thrift访问的端口配置。</span><span style="color:rgb(255,0,255); line-height:20px; white-space:pre; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)"><strong><span style="color:rgb(51,102,255)">thrift://192.168.1.214:9083</span></strong></span><span style="line-height:20px; white-space:pre; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)">就是<span style="font-family:arial; font-size:13px">hive元数据访问路径</span>。</span><br>
</span></div>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"><span style="line-height:20px; white-space:pre; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)"><br>
</span></span></div>
进入hive客户端，运行show tables;</div>
<div style="font-size:14.2857151031494px"><span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"><br>
</span></div>
</div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">
<span style="line-height:22.8571434020996px"><span style="line-height:20px">至此，可以在linux用各种shell来测试，也可以通过eclipse连接到hive来测试，和通过jdbc连接普通数据库一致</span></span></div>
<div style="font-weight:normal; font-size:14.2857151031494px; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:20px">

<h1 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-weight:normal"><a target="_blank" name="t23" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a></h1>
<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-weight:normal; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<a target="_blank" name="t24" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">4.  与Hbase整合</span></span></p>

<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O2" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">

</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t25" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
<div style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div class="O" style="padding:0px; margin:0px auto; border-width:0px; overflow:hidden">
<p><span style="font-weight:normal"><span style="font-size:14px">之前我们测试创建表的都是<span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">创建本地表,非hbase对应表。现在我们整合回到hbase。</span></span></span></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t26" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>1.创建hbase识别的数据库：</h3>
<span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)"><span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)"></span></span>
<div class="dp-highlighter bg_plain" style="font-family:Consolas,'Courier New',Courier,mono,serif; border:1px dashed rgb(153,153,153); font-size:12px; width:700.90625px; overflow:auto; padding-top:1px; margin:18px 0px!important; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)">
<div class="bar" style="background-color:rgb(221,221,221)">
<div class="tools" style="padding:3px 8px 5px 10px; font-size:9px; line-height:normal; font-family:Verdana,Geneva,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; color:silver">
<strong>[plain]</strong> <a target="_blank" href="http://blog.csdn.net/hguisu/article/details/7282050#" rel="nofollow" class="ViewSource" title="view plain" style="color:rgb(85,85,85); text-decoration:none; border:none; padding:0px; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; background-color:inherit">view
 plain</a><a target="_blank" href="http://blog.csdn.net/hguisu/article/details/7282050#" rel="nofollow" class="CopyToClipboard" title="copy" style="color:rgb(85,85,85); text-decoration:none; border:none; padding:0px; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; background-color:inherit">copy</a><a target="_blank" href="http://blog.csdn.net/hguisu/article/details/7282050#" rel="nofollow" class="PrintSource" title="print" style="color:rgb(85,85,85); text-decoration:none; border:none; padding:0px; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; background-color:inherit">print</a><a target="_blank" href="http://blog.csdn.net/hguisu/article/details/7282050#" rel="nofollow" class="About" title="?" style="color:rgb(85,85,85); text-decoration:none; border:none; padding:0px; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; background-color:inherit">?</a><a target="_blank" href="https://code.csdn.net/snippets/183509" rel="nofollow" title="在CODE上查看代码片" style="color:rgb(85,85,85); text-decoration:none; border:none; padding:0px; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; background-color:inherit"><img src="https://code.csdn.net/assets/CODE_ico.png" width="12" height="12" alt="在CODE上查看代码片" style="border:none; max-width:100%; position:relative; top:1px; left:2px"></a><a target="_blank" href="https://code.csdn.net/snippets/183509/fork" rel="nofollow" title="派生到我的代码片" style="color:rgb(85,85,85); text-decoration:none; border:none; padding:0px; margin:0px 10px 0px 0px; font-size:9px; background-color:inherit"><img src="https://code.csdn.net/assets/ico_fork.svg" width="12" height="12" alt="派生到我的代码片" style="border:none; max-width:100%; position:relative; top:2px; left:2px"></a>
<div style="position:absolute; left:557px; top:10553px; width:27px; height:15px; z-index:99">
</div>
</div>
</div>
<ol start="1" style="margin:0px; padding:5px 0px; border:none; position:relative; list-style-position:initial; color:rgb(92,92,92)">
<li class="alt" style="margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; color:inherit; line-height:13.1999998092651px">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">CREATE TABLE hbase_table_1(key int, value string)  </span></li><li style="border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; line-height:13.1999998092651px; margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">STORED BY 'org.apache.hadoop.hive.hbase.HBaseStorageHandler'  </span></li><li class="alt" style="margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; color:inherit; line-height:13.1999998092651px">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">WITH SERDEPROPERTIES ("hbase.columns.mapping" = ":key,cf1:val")  </span></li><li style="border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; line-height:13.1999998092651px; margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">TBLPROPERTIES ("hbase.table.name" = "xyz");    </span></li></ol>
</div>
<p>hbase.table.name 定义在hbase的table名称</p>
<p>hbase.columns.mapping 定义在hbase的列族 </p>
<p><br>
</p>
<p><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">在hbase 下也能看到，两边新增数据都能实时看到。</span><br>
</p>
<p><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif">可以登录Hbase去查看数据了<br>
#bin/hbase shell<br>
<span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)"><span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">hbase(main):001:0&gt; describe 'xyz'  </span><br style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">
<span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">hbase(main):002:0&gt; scan 'xyz'  </span><br style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">
<span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">hbase(main):003:0&gt; put 'xyz','100','cf1:val','www.360buy.com'</span></span><br>
<br>
这时在Hive中可以看到刚才在Hbase中插入的数据了。</span></p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t27" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>2.使用sql导入数据</h3>
<div><br>
</div>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:18.25px">如果要insert 与hbase整合的表，不能像本地表一样load，需要利用已有的表进行。<small style="line-height:20px"><small><span style="font-size:13.9130439758301px; line-height:18.2608699798584px">如</span></small></small></span></div>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:18.25px"><span style="line-height:18.2589302062988px"><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">insert
 overwrite <span style="color:rgb(255,255,255); background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">hbase_table_1</span> hivetest select * from <span style="color:rgb(255,255,255); background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">pokes</span>  </span></span></span></div>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:18.25px"><span style="font-size:10.5pt; line-height:18.2589302062988px"><span style="color:rgb(51,102,255)"><strong>注意两个的类型要一致</strong></span>，否则用</span><span style="line-height:18.2589302062988px">insert
 overwrite table hivetest select * from table_hive; 导不进去数据</span></span><br>
</div>
<div><span style="font-family:'Microsoft YaHei UI','Microsoft YaHei',SimSun,'Segoe UI',Tahoma,Helvetica,sans-serif,'Microsoft YaHei',Georgia,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif,宋体,PMingLiU,serif; line-height:18.25px"><span style="line-height:18.2589302062988px"><br>
</span></span></div>
<p>使用sql导入hbase_table_1:</p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,255,255); background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">hive&gt; INSERT OVERWRITE TABLE hbase_table_1 SELECT * FROM pokes WHERE foo=86</span>; <br>
</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t28" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><br>
</h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px"><a target="_blank" name="t29" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>3 hive访问已经存在的hbase<br>
</h3>
<p>使用CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE:<br>
<span style="background-color:rgb(102,102,102)"></span></p>
<div class="dp-highlighter bg_plain" style="font-family:Consolas,'Courier New',Courier,mono,serif; border:1px dashed rgb(153,153,153); font-size:12px; width:700.90625px; overflow:auto; padding-top:1px; margin:18px 0px!important; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)">
<div class="bar" style="background-color:rgb(221,221,221)">
<div class="tools" style="padding:3px 8px 5px 10px; font-size:9px; line-height:normal; font-family:Verdana,Geneva,Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; color:silver">

<div style="position:absolute; left:557px; top:11253px; width:27px; height:15px; z-index:99">
</div>
</div>
</div>
<ol start="1" style="margin:0px; padding:5px 0px; border:none; position:relative; list-style-position:initial; color:rgb(92,92,92)">
<li class="alt" style="margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; color:inherit; line-height:13.1999998092651px">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE hbase_table_2(key int, value string)        </span></li><li style="border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; line-height:13.1999998092651px; margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">STORED BY 'org.apache.hadoop.hive.hbase.HBaseStorageHandler'  </span></li><li class="alt" style="margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important; border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; color:inherit; line-height:13.1999998092651px">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">WITH SERDEPROPERTIES ("hbase.columns.mapping" = "cf1:val")  </span></li><li style="border:none; list-style:decimal-leading-zero outside; line-height:13.1999998092651px; margin:0px!important; padding:0px 3px 0px 10px!important">
<span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; border:none; color:black; background-color:inherit">TBLPROPERTIES("hbase.table.name" = "some_existing_table");  </span></li></ol>
</div>
<p>内容参考：http://wiki.apache.org/hadoop/Hive/HBaseIntegration</p>
<p></p>
<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-weight:normal; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<a target="_blank" name="t30" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">5.  问题</span></span></p>

<p></p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">bin/hive 执行show tables 报错：</span></p>
<p>Unable to instantiate org.apache.hadoop.hive.metastore.HiveMetaStoreClient<br>
</p>
<p>如果是<span style="font-size:16px; background-color:rgb(250,250,250)">使用Derby数据库的安装方式，查看</span></p>
<p>&lt;property&gt;<br>
  &lt;name&gt;hive.metastore.warehouse.dir&lt;/name&gt;<br>
  &lt;value&gt;/hive/warehousedir&lt;/value&gt;<br>
  &lt;description&gt;location of default database for the warehouse&lt;/description&gt;<br>
&lt;/property&gt;<br>
</p>
<p>配置是否正确，<br>
</p>
<p>或者<br>
<br>
&lt;property&gt;<br>
  &lt;name&gt;javax.jdo.option.ConnectionURL&lt;/name&gt;<br>
  &lt;value&gt;jdbc:derby:;databaseName=metastore_db;create=true&lt;/value&gt;<br>
  &lt;description&gt;JDBC connect string for a JDBC metastore&lt;/description&gt;<br>
&lt;/property&gt;<br>
</p>
<p>是否有权限访问。</p>
<p>如果<span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif; line-height:24px; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)">配置了mysql的Metastore方式,检查的权限：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif; line-height:24px; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)"> bin/hive  -hiveconf hive.root.logger=DEBUG,console  <br>
</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif; line-height:24px; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)">然后show tables 就会看到ava.sql.SQLException: Access denied for user 'hive'@'××××8' (using password: YES) 之类从错误消息。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif; line-height:24px; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)"><br>
</span></p>
<p><br>
</p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">执行</span></p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">CREATE TABLE hbase_table_1(key int, value string)  <br>
STORED BY 'org.apache.hadoop.hive.hbase.HBaseStorageHandler'  <br>
WITH SERDEPROPERTIES ("hbase.columns.mapping" = ":key,cf1:val")  <br>
TBLPROPERTIES ("hbase.table.name" = "xyz");</span></p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">报错：</span></p>
<p>FAILED: Execution Error, return code 1 from org.apache.hadoop.hive.ql.exec.DDLTask. MetaException(message:org.apache.hadoop.hbase.MasterNotRunningException: Retried 10 times<br>
</p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif; line-height:25.2000007629395px">出现这个错误的原因是引入的hbase包和hive自带的hive包冲突，删除hive/lib下的 hbase-0.94.×××.jar， OK了。</span><br>
</p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:25.2000007629395px">同时也要移走hive-0.12**.jar 包。</span></span></p>
<p><br>
</p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">执行</span></p>
<p><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">hive&gt;<span style="line-height:25.2000007629395px; font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif">select uid from user limit 100;</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:25.2000007629395px">java.io.IOException: Cannot initialize Cluster. Please check your configuration for mapreduce.framework.name and the correspond server addresses.<br>
</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:25.2000007629395px"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
解决：修改$HIVE_HOME/conf/hive-env<span style="background-color:rgb(255,153,153)">.</span>sh文件，加入</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
export HADOOP_HOME=hadoop的安装目录</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<br>
</p>
<br>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:25.2000007629395px"></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-weight:normal; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<a target="_blank" name="t31" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>
</h2><p class="headline-1 bk-sidecatalog-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:6px; border-bottom-color:rgb(222,223,225); border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; clear:both">
<span style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"><span style="line-height:36px; font-size:22px">5.  通过thrift访问hive（使用php做客户端）</span></span></p>

<p></p>
<p><a target="_blank" href="http://blog.csdn.net/jiedushi/article/details/6579285" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(51,51,51); text-decoration:none; font-family:'Microsoft YaHei'; line-height:30px"><strong>php连接hive执行sql查询</strong></a></p>
<p><span style="font-family:Helvetica,Tahoma,Arial,sans-serif"><span style="line-height:25.2000007629395px"></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<strong>使用php连接hive的条件：</strong></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<strong><br>
</strong></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<strong></strong></p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t32" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>1. 下载thrift</h3>
<p></p>
<p style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">wget http://mirror.bjtu.edu.cn/apache//thrift/0.9.1/thrift-0.9.1.tar.gz</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px"><a target="_blank" name="t33" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><a target="_blank" name="t3" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><span style="font-size:14px"></span></h3>
<h3 style="margin:0px; padding:0px; display:inline!important"><a target="_blank" name="t34" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>2. 解压</h3>
<p style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border-width:0px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; outline-width:0px; vertical-align:baseline; background-color:transparent">
tar -xzf thrift-0.9.1.tar.gz<br>
</p>
<h3 style="margin:0px 0px 20px; padding:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; border-width:0px; outline-width:0px; font-size:14px; vertical-align:baseline; background-color:transparent">
<a target="_blank" name="t35" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a><a target="_blank" name="t4" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>3 .编译安装：</h3>
<p style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border-width:0px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; outline-width:0px; vertical-align:baseline; background-color:transparent">
如果是源码编译的，首先要使用./boostrap.sh创建文件./configure ，我们这下载的tar包，自带有configure文件了。(（可以查阅README文件）)<br>
</p>
<p style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border-width:0px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; outline-width:0px; vertical-align:baseline; background-color:rgb(102,102,102)">
<span style="color:rgb(255,255,255)">If you are building from the first time out of the source repository, you will<br>
need to generate the configure scripts.  (This is not necessary if you<br>
downloaded a tarball.)  From the top directory, do:<br>
./bootstrap.sh</span></p>
<p style="font-family:Arial; line-height:26px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border-width:0px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; outline-width:0px; vertical-align:baseline; background-color:transparent">
./configure</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
1  需要安装thrift  安装步骤</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
#  ./configure --without-ruby </p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
不要使用ruby，</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:20px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; border-width:0px; outline-width:0px; vertical-align:baseline; background-color:transparent">
make ; make install</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
如果没有安装libevent libevent-devel的应该先安装这两个依赖库yum -y install libevent libevent-devel</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
其实Thrift就是使用来生成客户端和服务器端代码的。在这里没用到。</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<br>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<strong>安装好后启动hive thrift</strong></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
# ./hive --service hiveserver &gt;/dev/null 2&gt;/dev/null &amp;</p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<strong><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)">查看hiveserver默认端口是否打开10000   如果打开表示成功，在官网wiki有介绍文章：https://cwiki.apache.org/confluence/display/Hive/HiveServer</span></strong></p>
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial; line-height:26px">
<strong><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0)"></span></strong></p>
<h1 id="HiveServer-ThriftHiveServer" style="margin:0px; padding:0px; font-size:24px; font-weight:normal; line-height:1.25; border-bottom-color:rgb(204,204,204); font-family:Arial,sans-serif">
<a target="_blank" name="t36" style="color:rgb(51,102,153)"></a>Thrift Hive Server</h1>
<p></p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; line-height:20px">
HiveServer is an optional service that allows a remote <a target="_blank" href="https://cwiki.apache.org/confluence/display/Hive/HiveClient" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(59,115,175); text-decoration:none">client</a> to submit requests to Hive, using a variety
 of programming languages, and retrieve results. HiveServer is built on Apache Thrift<sup>TM</sup>(<a target="_blank" href="http://thrift.apache.org/" rel="nofollow" class="external-link" style="color:rgb(59,115,175); text-decoration:none">http://thrift.apache.org/</a>),
 therefore it is sometimes called the <em>Thrift server</em> although this can lead to confusion because a newer service named <a target="_blank" href="https://cwiki.apache.org/confluence/display/Hive/Setting+Up+HiveServer2#SettingUpHiveServer2-HiveServer2" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(59,115,175); text-decoration:none">HiveServer2</a> is
 also built on Thrift.</p>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; line-height:20px">
Thrift's interface definition language (IDL) file for HiveServer is <span style="color:rgb(34,34,34)"><code>hive_service.thrift</code>, which is installed in <code>$HIVE_HOME/service/if/</code>.</span></p>
<div class="aui-message problem shadowed information-macro">
<p class="title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-weight:bold">WARNING!</p>
<span class="aui-icon icon-problem" style="">Icon</span>
<div class="message-content">
<p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px">HiveServer cannot handle concurrent requests from more than one client. This is actually a limitation imposed by the Thrift interface that HiveServer exports, and can't be resolved by modifying the HiveServer code.<br>
<a target="_blank" href="https://cwiki.apache.org/confluence/display/Hive/HiveServer2+Clients" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(59,115,175); text-decoration:none">HiveServer2</a> is a rewrite of HiveServer that addresses these problems, starting with Hive 0.11.0.
 See <a target="_blank" href="https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/HIVE-2935" rel="nofollow" class="external-link" style="color:rgb(59,115,175); text-decoration:none">HIVE-2935</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<p style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; line-height:20px">
Once Hive has been built using steps in <a target="_blank" href="https://cwiki.apache.org/confluence/display/Hive/GettingStarted" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(59,115,175); text-decoration:none">Getting Started</a>, the Thrift server can be started by running
 the following:</p>
<div class="code panel pdl" style="margin:10px 0px; padding:0px; border:1px solid rgb(204,204,204); overflow:auto; font-family:Arial,sans-serif; line-height:20px">
<div class="codeHeader panelHeader pdl" style="padding:5px 15px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-bottom-style:solid; border-bottom-color:rgb(204,204,204); overflow:hidden; position:relative; background-color:rgb(245,245,245)">
<strong>0.8 and Later</strong></div>
<div class="codeContent panelContent pdl" style="padding:0px; margin:0px; overflow:hidden">
<div id="highlighter_620220" class="syntaxhighlighter nogutter  bash" style="width:1336px; margin:0px!important; position:relative!important; overflow:auto!important; font-size:1em!important">
<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:1336px; border:0px!important; bottom:auto!important; float:none!important; height:auto!important; left:auto!important; line-height:20px!important; margin:0px!important; outline:0px!important; overflow:visible!important; padding:0px!important; position:static!important; right:auto!important; top:auto!important; vertical-align:baseline!important; font-family:Consolas,'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono','Courier New',Courier,monospace!important; font-size:14px!important; min-height:inherit!important">
<tbody style="border:0px!important; bottom:auto!important; float:none!important; height:auto!important; left:auto!important; margin:0px!important; outline:0px!important; overflow:visible!important; padding:0px!important; position:static!important; right:auto!important; top:auto!important; vertical-align:baseline!important; width:auto!important; min-height:inherit!important">
<tr style="border:0px!important; bottom:auto!important; float:none!important; height:auto!important; left:auto!important; margin:0px!important; outline:0px!important; overflow:visible!important; padding:0px!important; position:static!important; right:auto!important; top:auto!important; vertical-align:baseline!important; width:auto!important; min-height:inherit!important">
<td class="code" style="width:1321px; border:0px!important; overflow:visible!important; bottom:auto!important; float:none!important; height:auto!important; left:auto!important; margin:0px!important; outline:0px!important; padding:0px 0px 0px 15px!important; position:static!important; right:auto!important; top:auto!important; vertical-align:baseline!important; font-family:Consolas,'Bitstream Vera Sans Mono','Courier New',Courier,monospace!important; font-size:14px!important; min-height:inherit!important">
